2025-06-01T02:08:15.6365734Z         If you don't want 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' to be distributed and are
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6365897Z         already explicitly excluding 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' via
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366074Z         `find_namespace_packages(...)/find_namespace` or `find_packages(...)/find`,
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366247Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366408Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366413Z 
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366595Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366604Z 
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366768Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366773Z 
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366777Z 
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6366977Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6367170Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6367640Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T02:08:15.6367885Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
